:PROPERTIES:
:TX_ID:        tx-20260703-orgasmic-1259
:TIME:         [2026-07-03 Fri 21:33:52]

:MACHINE:      Vasyls-MacBook-Pro.local
:PROJECT:      orgasmic
:TASK:         TASK-Y2ZQJ
:TARGET:       crates/orgasmic-daemon/src/api.rs
:REASON:       M1 MEDIUM regression (data loss): the finding-#4 atomicity fix replaced writer.mutate_file(FileMutate{transform}) — which read reviews.org INSIDE the writer flock (serialized read-modify-write) — with read-OUTSIDE-lock (std::fs::read_to_string) -> compute append_comment -> blind FileRewrite overwrite via writer.transaction. Two concurrent comment-add/consume ops on the same artifact both read the same base and the second silently clobbers the first, losing a comment or a consume. Gained atomicity, lost serialization. Fix: add a writer transactional-RMW primitive (read-under-flock + transform + tx-append committed together) and route post_artifact_feedback / post_artifact_feedback_consume through it, or guard the read->transaction window with a per-artifact mutex. Should be fixed before the artifact queue drives concurrency onto the store.
:severity:     medium
:kind:         regression
:run:          run-20260703T211936
:locations:    api.rs:9051+9095 (feedback add); api.rs:9143+9186 (consume)
:END:

:TASK:         TASK-2ZQSB
:TARGET:       crates/orgasmic-daemon/src/api.rs
:REASON:       M1 MEDIUM (pre-existing, surfaced by 2ZQSB): post_artifact_submit's existing-artifact read->transaction (read version/state from artifact.org, archive vN, write version+1) is NOT under the per-artifact artifact_write_lock. Two concurrent submits race on the version (lost update), and submit races regenerate's state read/flip. The Y2ZQJ M1 lock covered feedback add/consume but not submit; 2ZQSB makes it more reachable (regenerate flips state, worker submits concurrently with possible comment activity). Fix: wrap post_artifact_submit's existing-artifact read->transaction in state.artifact_write_lock(&art_dir), matching feedback/regenerate.
:severity:     medium
:kind:         concurrency
:preexisting:  true
:run:          run-20260703T233904
:END:
